# Argus Startup

##General Fix to 18.2 M&C system
##Resets all configuration values to defaults
##important after KFPA projects using frequency dictionary
ResetConfig()

print "CIF Power:", GetValue("RcvrArray75_115","cif_power")
print "LNA Power:", GetValue("RcvrArray75_115","lna_power")

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.6

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

Catalog(projectDir+"/GBTEDGE.cat") 

print "Mapping galaxy: ", galaxyName
print "Integration time per row (s): ", mymap['scanDuration']
print "Offset between map rows (arcsec): ", mymap['step']
print "Length of scan (arcmin): ", mymap['scanLength']
print "Height of map (arcmin): ", mymap['mapHeight']

Configure(argus_config)
execfile(projectDir+"/addwx.py")

Slew(galaxyName)
Balance()

execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

DecLatMap( galaxyName,
           Offset("J2000", mymap['mapHeight']/60., 0.0, cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", 0.0, mymap['scanLength']/60., cosv=True),
           Offset("J2000", mymap['step']/3600., 0.0, cosv=True),
           scanDuration=mymap['scanDuration'], beamName='C')

	   # can add start and stop row parameters to the above, 
	   # e.g., start=2, stop=13


execfile("/home/astro-util/projects/Argus/OBS/argus_vanecal")

#load catalogs

Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.6

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig()

#load catalogs

deltaFocus=5.6

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.6

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."

#load catalogs
#Catalog(qband_pointing)
#Catalog(wband_pointing)
Catalog(xband_pointing)
#Catalog(fluxcal)
Catalog(projectDir+"/alma_fluxcal_grid.cat")

# choose appropriate source
source = pointSrc
#focus offset parameter (add to KFPA value for Argus)
deltaFocus=5.6

Slew(source)

Break("Ask the operator to switch the receiver to KFPA (RcvrArray18_26).  Click yes when KFPA  is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray18_26"})
## may want to set LO frequency here

SetValues("LO1",{"restFrequency_A":25000})

AutoPeak(source,configure=True) 

Break("enter pointing offsets")

Focus(source) 

# adjust the focus properly for Argus
lfc = float(GetValue("Antenna", "local_focus_correction,Y"))
new_lfc = lfc +deltaFocus
SetValues("Antenna", {"local_focus_correction,Y": new_lfc})

Comment("")
Comment("-------------------------------")
Comment("LFC changed  from %f  to  %f     (shift of %f  mm)"  %(float(lfc), float(new_lfc), float(deltaFocus)))
Comment("--------------------------------")
Comment("")
Break("enter focus values if necessary")

Break ("Ask the operator to switch back to Argus. Click yes when Argus is in place.")

SetValues("ScanCoordinator", {"receiver": "RcvrArray75_115"})

# ResetConfig() 

#configure Argus
Configure(argus_config)
print "Setting up the YIG filter and LO for Argus during the operator switch from X-band to Argus."
